 Let us know that India Sports Flashes Private Limited is an organization which has rights to broadcast live audio feed of ICC World Cup on app and web platform
 india sports flashes privet limited ne dilli hoicourt ke samaksh kaha ki sports broadcasting signal (prasar bharti ke saath anivaary sajhakaran) act 2007 ke anusaar, ve rashtriya mahatv ke kisi bhi khel kii radio camentry tab tak prasaarit nahin kar sakate jab tak ki wo prasar bharti ke saath (ek saath, bina kisi samay antaraal ke) live prasaaran signal saajha na karen
 Consider it in other words that as per the rule, India Sports Flashes Private Limited will also have to share the live broadcast signal to Prasar Bharati in order to broadcast the World Cup radio commentary
 act kii dhara 3 ke ek sab cloj ke mutabik, 'niyam or sharton ke mutabik live prasaaran ke dauraan vigyaapan se hone vaali kamai kaa bantwaaraa aadhikarik malikana (swami yaa dharak) rakhane vaali sanstha or prasar bharti ke bich televijan kawarej ke maamle main 75:25 ke anupaat se kam nahin hoga
 In the case of radio coverage it will not be less than the ratio of 50:50
 'prasar bharti ne yachikakarta dwaara hoicourt main di gai jaankaree ko chunauti di, jisamen kaha gaya ki sports flashes privet limited is tarah kii sevaayen (match kaa live prasaaran) pradaan karne ke liye na to radio channel he or na hi licensadhari he
